In this movement, the projectiles are launched and subjected to a downward  constant acceleration due to the force of gravity, causing the projectiles to describe a parabolic trajectory. Within the study of projectile motion, the determination of the range and its relation with the angle of launch are also very important.\r\nSeeking to approach the concepts contained in the projectile movement, this simulator brings two scenarios, each one with different gravity values: the Earth and the Moon.
